<h1 _ngcontent-wpd-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@arkts.math.Decimal (高精度数学库Decimal)"> @arkts.math.Decimal (高精度数学库Decimal) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-wpd-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>Decimal用于提供高精度数学运算的能力，支持高精度浮点计算。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 12开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>      <p>此模块仅支持在ArkTS文件（文件后缀为.ets）中导入使用。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-wpd-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-wpd-c106="" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Value<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="value" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>type Value = string | number | Decimal</p>     <p>表示用于构建Decimal的参数类型。</p>     <p>取值类型为下列类型中的并集。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.4.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示值类型为字符串，可取任意值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示值类型为数字，可取任意值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#decimal">Decimal</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">表示值类型为Decimal类型。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1057px;">     <h2 id="rounding" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Rounding<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="rounding" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>type Rounding = 0 | 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5 | 6 | 7 | 8</p>     <p>表示可设置的舍入类型。</p>     <p>取值类型为下列类型中的并集。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">向远离零的方向舍入。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Decimal.ROUND_UP</a>一致。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">向靠近零的方向舍入。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Decimal.ROUND_DOWN</a>一致。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">向正无穷方向舍入。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Decimal.ROUND_CEILING</a>一致。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">3</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">向负无穷方向舍入。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Decimal.ROUND_FLOOR</a>一致。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">4</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">向最近的邻值舍入。如果距离相等，则远离零方向舍入。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Decimal.ROUND_HALF_UP</a>一致。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">5</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">向最近的邻值舍入。如果距离相等，则靠近零方向舍入。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Decimal.ROUND_HALF_DOWN</a>一致。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">6</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">向最近的邻值舍入。如果距离相等，则向偶数邻值舍入。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Decimal.ROUND_HALF_EVEN</a>一致。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">7</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">向最近的邻值舍入。如果距离相等，则向正无穷方向舍入。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Decimal.ROUND_HALF_CEILING</a>一致。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">8</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">向最近的邻值舍入。如果距离相等，则向负无穷方向舍入。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Decimal.ROUND_HALF_FLOOR</a>一致。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 576px;">     <h2 id="modulo" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Modulo<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="modulo" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>type Modulo = Rounding | 9</p>     <p>表示可设置的取模方法舍入类型。</p>     <p>取值类型为下列类型中的并集。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#rounding">Rounding</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">模运算下的舍入类型。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Rounding</a>表示的舍入模式相同。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">9</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">余模运算下，余数始终为正。欧几里得除法，与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#常量">Decimal.EUCLIDEAN</a>一致。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 182px;">     <h2 id="decimalconfig" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">DecimalConfig<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="decimalconfig" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>用于设置Decimal的配置属性，可使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#set">Decimal.set</a>方法进行配置。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1653px;">     <h3 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">属性<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="属性" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.4.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.4.1.6.1.2" width="20%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.4.1.6.1.3" width="20%">只读</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.4.1.6.1.4" width="20%">可选</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.8.4.1.6.1.5" width="20%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">precision</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">运算结果的最大有效位数，取值范围为[1, 1e9]，默认值为20。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">rounding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#rounding">Rounding</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">舍入模式，取值范围为0到8的整数，默认值为4。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">toExpNeg</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">指数表示法的负指数值的极限值，若Decimal的负指数小于等于该值时，使用科学计数法表示，<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#tostring">toString</a>方法中使用，取值范围为[-9e15, 0]，默认值为-7。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">toExpPos</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">指数表示法的正指数值的极限值，若Decimal的正指数大于等于该值时，使用科学计数法表示，<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#tostring">toString</a>方法中使用，取值范围为[0, 9e15]，默认值为21。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">minE</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">负指数极限，若Decimal的指数值小于该值，会下溢到零，取值范围为[-9e15, 0]，默认值为-9e15。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">maxE</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">正指数极限，若Decimal的指数值大于该值，会溢出至无穷大，取值范围为[0, 9e15]，默认值为9e15。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">crypto</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">确定是否使用加密安全伪随机数生成的值，true表示使用加密安全伪随机数，false表示不使用，默认值为false。该能力不支持使用，报错的错误码为：10200061。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">modulo</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#modulo">Modulo</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">模计算时使用的舍入模式，取值范围为0到9的整数，默认值为1。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">defaults</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">表示未指定的属性是否被设置为默认值，true表示使用默认值，false表示不使用默认值，默认值为true。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.4.1.5.1.1" width="25%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.4.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.4.1.5.1.3" width="25%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.4.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ROUND_UP</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">向远离零的方向舍入。模运算下，如果被除数为负，则余数为正，否则为负。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ROUND_DOWN</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">向靠近零的方向舍入。模运算下，余数与被除数的符号相同，使用截断除法。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ROUND_CEILING</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">2</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">向正无穷方向舍入。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ROUND_FLOOR</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">3</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">向负无穷方向舍入。模运算下，余数与除数的符号相同。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ROUND_HALF_UP</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">4</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">向最近的邻值舍入。如果距离相等，则向远离零的方向舍入。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ROUND_HALF_DOWN</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">5</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">向最近的邻值舍入。如果距离相等，则向靠近零方向舍入。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ROUND_HALF_EVEN</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">6</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">向最近的邻值舍入。如果距离相等，则向偶数邻值舍入。模运算下，IEEE 754 求余函数。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ROUND_HALF_CEILING</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">7</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">向最近的邻值舍入。如果距离相等，则向正无穷方向舍入。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ROUND_HALF_FLOOR</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">8</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">向最近的邻值舍入。如果距离相等，则向负无穷方向舍入。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">EUCLIDEAN</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">9</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">模运算下，余数始终为正。使用欧几里得除法：q = sign(x) * floor(a / abs(x))。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>  </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1336px;">     <h3 id="clamp" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">clamp<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="clamp" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>clamp(min: Value, max: Value): Decimal</p>     <p>返回一个将Decimal值限制在min到max范围内的Decimal对象。如果值大于max，返回max；如果值小于min，返回min；否则，返回原值。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">min</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a width="25%">限制的最小值。包含该值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">max</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a width="25%">限制的最大值。包含该值。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.17.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a 1116px;">     <h3 id="add" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">add<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon Value): Decimal</p>     <p>返回一个新的Decimal对象，其值是将此Decimal的值加上n。</p>     <p>使用<a <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th      </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>返回该Decimal与n的比较结果：</p> <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">n</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a      </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>toBinary(significantDigits: number, rounding: Rounding): string</p>     <p>将Decimal转换为二进制表示的字符串，并可按照significantDigits设置有效数字，以及按照rounding设置舍入模式。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.57.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.57.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.57.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.57.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">significantDigits</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">转换时保留的有效数字，取值范围为[1, 1e9]的整数。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">rounding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#rounding">Rounding</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">转换时使用的舍入模式，取值范围参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#rounding">Rounding</a>。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回二进制表示的字符串。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>toDecimalPlaces(decimalPlaces: number, rounding: Rounding): Decimal</p>     <p>返回一个保留小数点后指定位数的Decimal对象，可按照decimalPlaces设置小数位数，可按照rounding设置舍入模式。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">decimalPlaces</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">转换时保留的小数点后有效位数，取值范围为[0, 1e9]的整数。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">rounding</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#rounding">Rounding</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">转换时使用的舍入模式。取值范围参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#rounding">Rounding</a>。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> string</p>     <p>将数值转换为十进制定点模式表示的字符串，不进行小数的取舍。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p> class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回按照正常模式（十进制定点模式）表示的字符串。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#decimalconfig">toExpPos</a>，或负指数等于或小于<a width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回一个表示Decimal的字符串。</td>        </tr> id="precision-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">precision<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="precision-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>precision(includeZeros: boolean | number): number</p>     <p>返回Decimal对象的有效数字位数，通过includeZeros判断是否计算整数部分的尾随零。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.88.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.88.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.88.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.88.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">includeZeros</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean | number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是否计算整数部分尾随零。true或1表示计算整数部分尾随零，false或0表示不计算整数部分尾随零。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回Decimal对象的有效位数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-utils">语言基础类库错误码</a>。</p>  </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1237px;">     <h3 id="clamp-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">clamp<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="clamp-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static clamp(n: Value, min: Value, max: Value): Decimal</p>     <p>返回一个值为将该Decimal的值限制在min到max范围内的Decimal对象，当大于限制的最大值时返回max，小于限制的最小值时返回min，在范围内返回值不变。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Utils.Lang</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.93.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.93.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.93.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.93.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">n</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#decimalconfig">DecimalConfig.rounding</a>的值设置舍入模式。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.120.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.120.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">y</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#value">Value</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">除法的被除数。</td>      </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#decimal">Decimal</a></td>         <td device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">hypot<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="hypot" hypot(...n: Value[]): Decimal</p>     <p>返回一个新的Decimal对象，其值是参数平方和的平方根。无入参时默认返回0。</p>     <p>使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#decimalconfig">DecimalConfig.precision</a>的值进行有效数字的保留，使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-arkts-decimal#decimalconfig">DecimalConfig.rounding</a>的值设置舍入模式。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">sign<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="sign" sign(n: Value): number</p>     <p>根据参数的值进行判断返回对应的值：当n&gt;0返回1，当n&lt;0返回-1，当n==0返回0，当n==-0返回-0，否则返回NaN。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API</strong>：从API version 12 开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p> </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">n</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a
